SELECT `availableCar0`.`Id`, `availableCar0`.`CarId`, `availableCar0`.`NumberOfCars`, `availableCar0`.`Price`, `booking0`.`Id`, `booking0`.`AvailableCarId`, `booking0`.`From`, `booking0`.`To`, `booking0`.`UserId`, `car0`.`Id`, `car0`.`Name`, `car0`.`TransmissionType`, `car0`.`NumberOfDoors`, `car0`.`NumberOfBags`, `car0`.`NumberOfSeats`, `car0`.`HasPetrol`, `car0`.`HasDiesel`, `car0`.`HasAirConditioning`, `car0`.`ImageUrl`, `carType0`.`Id`, `carType0`.`Type`
FROM `AvailableCars` AS `availableCar0`
INNER JOIN `Cars` AS `car0` ON `availableCar0`.`CarId` = `car0`.`Id`
INNER JOIN `CarTypes` AS `carType0` ON `car0`.`TypeId` = `carType0`.`Id`

INNER JOIN `Cars` AS `car0` ON `availableCar0`.`CarId` = `car0`.`Id`
INNER JOIN `CarTypes` AS `carType0` ON `car0`.`TypeId` = `carType0`.`Id`

INNER JOIN `CarTypes` AS `carType0` ON `car0`.`TypeId` = `carType0`.`Id`

ORDER BY `availableCar0`.`Id`
